 The Ministry of Railways has decided to implement the Flexi Fair system in Duronto, Rajdhani and Shatabdi
 iske tahat 10 fisadi seat book hone par base fere main 10 fisadi kaa ijapha ho jayega
 This preparation of the railway is being done to overcome the ghat
 is system ke tahat in sabhi trainon main uplabdh siton main se 10 fisadi siton kii booking mul kiraye par hogi
 That is, if the original fare of a place is Rs 100, then the first 10 per cent tickets will be booked at the base price of Rs 100
 10 fisadi siton kii booking ke baad rajdhani or duranton ke agle 10 fisadi tikat 110 rupee ke aadhaar par book honge
